<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкатывать.html>подка́тывать</a> (17825)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкатить.html>подкати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podkatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкатывать.html>подка́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкатить.html>подкати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll <i>(to)</i>, to drive <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to roll up <i>(to)</i>, to drive up <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><i>(emotions)</i> to rise <i>(in)</i>, to fill, to seize</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкачать.html>подкача́ть</a> (23310)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kačátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкачать.html>подкача́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkačátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подка́чивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pump up; to inflate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to let down; to disappoint
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podvestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочаровать.html>разочарова́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razočarovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***подкидывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкидывать.html>подки́дывать</a> (20600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подки́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podkíd-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкидывать.html>подки́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkídyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкинуть.html>подки́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to toss up, to throw up</li>
<li>to throw <i>(under)</i></li>
<li>to put secretly/stealthily, to plant <i>(a fake evidence)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подкидывать.html>подки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнка</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podkídyvatʹ</b> rebjónka komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to abandon a baby at smb's door</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to add
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подкидывать.html>подки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрова.html>дро́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печка.html>пе́чку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podkídyvatʹ</b> drov v péčku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw more (fire)wood on the fire</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give a lift</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bring up, to give some more
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подкидывать.html>подки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:резерв.html>резе́рвы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podkídyvatʹ</b> rezérvy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw in one's reserves</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to add <i>(a card)</i> to be beaten</li></ol>

***подкинуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкинуть.html>подки́нуть</a> (9381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуть.html>ки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкинуть.html>подки́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкидывать.html>подки́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to toss up, to throw up</li>
<li>to throw <i>(under)</i></li>
<li>to put secretly/stealthily, to plant <i>(fake evidence)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подкинуть.html>подки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнка</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podkínutʹ</b> rebjónka komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to abandon a baby at someone's door</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to add
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подкинуть.html>подки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрова.html>дро́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печка.html>пе́чку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podkínutʹ</b> drov v péčku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw more (fire)wood on the fire</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give a lift</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bring up, to give some more
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подкинуть.html>подки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньжата.html>деньжа́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podkínutʹ</b> denʹžát</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give some more money</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to add <i>(a card)</i> to be beaten</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкидыш.html>подки́дыш</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podkídyš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подкидно́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podkidnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***подкладка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкладка.html>подкла́дка</a> (15574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + a deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:класть.html>класть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klastʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to put, lay down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкладка.html>подкла́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkládka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкладка.html>подкла́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкладка.html>подкла́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкладка.html>подкла́док</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>backing <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">material added behind or underneath</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>lining, cushion</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкладывать.html>подкла́дывать</a> (12179)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кла́дывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкладывать.html>подкла́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkládyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подложить.html>подложи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lay <i>(under)</i>, to put <i>(under)</i></li>
<li>to line <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to add, to put some more</li>
<li>to put/place furtively, to plant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подкладывать.html>подкла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свинья.html>свинью́</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podkládyvatʹ</b> svinʹjú komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to play a mean/dirty trick on/upon someone; do the dirty on someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***подключать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подключать.html>подключа́ть</a> (23720)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключить.html>подключи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключать.html>подключа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podključátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключить.html>подключи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to connect <i>(to)</i>, to link up <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подключённый.html>подключённом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:режим.html>режи́ме</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v podključónnom režíme</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on line</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключённый.html>подключённое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устройство.html>устро́йство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podključónnoje ustrójstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on-line unit</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to enable, to turn on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подключать.html>подключа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:питание.html>пита́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podključátʹ</b> k pitániju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to power up; turn on power supply <i>(to)</i></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get involved <i>(in)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подключаться.html>подключа́ться</a> (19727)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключать.html>подключа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podključátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключаться.html>подключа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podključátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключиться.html>подключи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to connect <i>(to)</i>, to make a connection <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подключаться.html>подключа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:линия.html>ли́нии</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́лях</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прослушивание.html>прослу́шивания</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podključátʹsja</b> k línii (v céljax proslúšivanija)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to listen in on a line; tap a line/wire</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get involved <i>(in)</i>, to join in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подключаться.html>подключа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беседа.html>бесе́де</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podključátʹsja</b> k beséde</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to join in the conversation</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключать.html>подключа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podključátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключить.html>подключи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podključítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключать.html>подключа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to connect <i>(to)</i>, to link up <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подключённый.html>подключённом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:режим.html>режи́ме</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v podključónnom režíme</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on line</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключённый.html>подключённое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устройство.html>устро́йство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podključónnoje ustrójstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on-line unit</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to enable, to turn on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подключить.html>подключи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:питание.html>пита́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podključítʹ</b> k pitániju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to power up; turn on power supply <i>(to)</i></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get involved <i>(in)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подключиться.html>подключи́ться</a> (16777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключить.html>подключи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключиться.html>подключи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podključítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключаться.html>подключа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to connect <i>(to)</i>, to make a connection <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подключиться.html>подключи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:линия.html>ли́нии</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́лях</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прослушивание.html>прослу́шивания</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podključítʹsja</b> k línii (v céljax proslúšivanija)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to listen in on a line; tap a line/wire</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get involved <i>(in)</i>, to join in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подключиться.html>подключи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беседа.html>бесе́де</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podključítʹsja</b> k beséde</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to join in the conversation</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключить.html>подключи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключать.html>подключа́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podključátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подключить.html>подключи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***подкожный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкожный.html>подко́жный</a> (13659)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">under, sub-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóža</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкожный.html>подко́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkóžnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>subcutaneous, hypodermic</li></ol>

***подкоп.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкоп.html>подко́п</a> (24008)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подкопа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podkopátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкоп.html>подко́п</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkóp</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкоп.html>подко́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкоп.html>подко́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкоп.html>подко́пов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>underground passage, tunnel <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dug in the earth</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <span class="deprecated-label">usually in the plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> intrigue</li></ol>

***подкосить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкосить.html>подкоси́ть</a> (24271)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:косить.html>коси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kosítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкосить.html>подкоси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подка́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cut (grass, etc.) with a scythe</li>
<li>to mow at the base</li>
<li>to mow <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a little or additionally</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to knock down <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with a blow or shot</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause (legs or knees) to buckle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deprive of health, to energy, to stamina, etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to undermine, to undercut, to weaken</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкрадываться.html>подкра́дываться</a> (16174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкрасться.html>подкра́сться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podkrástʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкрадываться.html>подкра́дываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkrádyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкрасться.html>подкра́сться</a></b>)

***подкрасить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкрасить.html>подкра́сить</a> (23682)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красить.html>кра́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krásitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкрасить.html>подкра́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkrásitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкрашивать.html>подкра́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to touch up (something with paint, dye or makeup)</li>
<li>to paint (something) more</li>
<li>to tint</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to beautify, to embellish</li></ol>
